<p style=3D'margin:0in;font-family:"210 맨발의청춘 B";font-size:22.0pt=
;color:#2E75B5'><span
lang=3Den-US># 5 Z-score scaling </span><span lang=3Dko>표준정규분포<=
/span><span
lang=3Den-US> </span><span lang=3Dko>정규화</span></p>
